\#define \hyperlink{minimal_8h_af64abdf9b0014e46b8228dbd5c8d49e5}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+V\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+S\+I\+T\+I\+O\+N}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em These values encode the bit positions of the decode position. These values can be used to read the value of a flag bit by combining the base\+\_\+mode variable with A\+N\+D with the flag position value. The result will be either 0 or 1, depending on if the flag is set or not. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

These values encode the bit positions of the decode position. These values can be used to read the value of a flag bit by combining the base\+\_\+mode variable with A\+N\+D with the flag position value. The result will be either 0 or 1, depending on if the flag is set or not.
